================================================================================
REAL EVALUATION v4 — STRONG PARADIGMS + LEARNED AGGREGATION + LLaMA 8B
================================================================================

KEY CHANGES FROM v3:
  1. Only 3 strong paradigms (dropped weak STS, Retrieval, Multi-QA, Lexical)
  2. Added LLM-as-Judge (Flan-T5) and QA verification (SQuAD 2.0)
  3. Calibration/evaluation split (30/70) for honest evaluation
  4. Learned meta-classifier (logistic regression) for optimal aggregation
  5. LLaMA 8B generator for E2E (instead of GPT-2)
